### rework by Simone - Traiano

focus_tree = {

	id = italy_focus

	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			tag = ITA
			add = 20
		}
	}

##SICK MAN OF EUROPE

	focus = {
		id = ITA_divided_nation
		icon = The_sick_man_of_Europe

		x = 15
		y = 0

		cost = 0.1

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_divided_nation"
			custom_effect_tooltip = list_of_statalist_parties_TT
		}

		ai_will_do = { base = 640 }
	}

##DIPLOMATIC FOCUS##

	focus = {
		id = ITA_diplomatic_focus
		icon = italy_deal

		x = 108
		y = 0

		cost = 0.1

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_NATO }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_diplomatic_focus"
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_diplomatic_focus_TT
		}

		ai_will_do = { base = 40 }
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_abandon_the_west
		icon = attack_nato

		x = -4
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = ITA_diplomatic_focus

		cost = 5

		prerequisite = { focus = ITA_diplomatic_focus }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west
			focus = ITA_strive_for_neutrality
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_NATO FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		available = { not_has_west_aligned_government = yes }

		bypass = { NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member } }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_abandon_the_west"
			NATO_leave = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_east_aligned_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west
		icon = align_to_nato

		x = 4
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = ITA_diplomatic_focus

		cost = 5

		prerequisite = { focus = ITA_diplomatic_focus }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = ITA_abandon_the_west
			focus = ITA_strive_for_neutrality
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_NATO FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		available = {
			not_has_east_aligned_government = yes
			has_idea = NATO_member
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west"
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.nato_members
				tooltip = TT_ALL_NATO_MEMBER_NATIONS_GAIN
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = reaffirmed_NATO }
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = reaffirmed_NATO }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = ITA_multipurpose_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_send_volunteer_divisions_required_var = -0.5 tooltip = send_volunteer_divisions_required_tt }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_send_volunteer_factor_var = 0.5 tooltip = send_volunteer_factor_tt }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_air_volunteer_cap_var = 50 tooltip = air_volunteer_cap_tt }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_east_aligned_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_west_aligned_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_strive_for_neutrality
		icon = ita_map_noglow

		x = 0
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = ITA_diplomatic_focus

		cost = 5

		prerequisite = { focus = ITA_diplomatic_focus }
		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = ITA_abandon_the_west
			focus = ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_NATO FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_strive_for_neutrality"
			custom_effect_tooltip = { localization_key = modifies_dynamic_modifier_tt MODIFIER = ITA_multipurpose_modifier }
			add_to_variable = { ITA_foreign_influence_defense_modifier_var = 0.1 tooltip = foreign_influence_defense_modifier_tt }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_east_aligned_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_west_aligned_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_draw_closer_to_east
		icon = align_to_russia

		x = -1
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = ITA_abandon_the_west

		cost = 2

		prerequisite = { focus = ITA_abandon_the_west }

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INFLUENCE }

		available = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } }

		bypass = { NOT = { country_exists = SOV } }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_draw_closer_to_east"
			SOV = {
				country_event = italy_md.44
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TT_IF_THEY_ACCEPT
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = medium_plane_fighter_airframe_1
						amount = 50
						producer = SOV
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = AS_Fighter2
						amount = 50
						producer = SOV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = medium_tank_amphibious_chassis_1
						amount = 1000
						producer = SOV
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = medium_tank_flame_chassis_0
						amount = 1000
						producer = SOV
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = APC_2
						amount = 1000
						producer = SOV
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = IFV_2
						amount = 1000
						producer = SOV
					}
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -75
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

						}
						set_temp_variable = { wargoal_on = wargoal_target }
						add_threat_from_wargoal_effect = yes
						create_wargoal = {
							type = take_claimed_state
							target = wargoal_target
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = { base = 20 }
	}
